delete from asset_service_schedule_params

drop table if exists #asset_master

create table #asset_master (
	[company_id] [varchar](20) NOT NULL,
	[country_code] [varchar](5) NOT NULL,
	[asset_id] [nvarchar](30) NOT NULL,
	[equipment_id] [nvarchar](30) NOT NULL,
	[customer_id] [nvarchar](30) NOT NULL,
	[customer_location_code] [nvarchar](30) NOT NULL,
	[company_location_code] [nvarchar](30) NOT NULL,
	[asset_category] [nvarchar](15) NOT NULL,
	[asset_type] [nvarchar](15) NOT NULL,
	[asset_status] [varchar](2) NOT NULL,
	[additional_information] [nvarchar](2000) NULL, 
	[asset_location_code] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[locator_layout] [nvarchar](30) NULL,
	[servicing_org_level_no] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
	[servicing_org_level_code] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	[installation_date] [datetimeoffset](7) NULL,
	[installation_job_ref_no] [nvarchar](30) NULL,
	[installation_by_org_level_no] [tinyint] NULL,
	[installation_by_org_level_code] [varchar](30) NULL,
	[oem_invoice_no] [nvarchar] (60) NULL,
	[oem_invoice_date] [datetimeoffset](7) NULL,
	[oem_invoiced_by_org_level_no] [tinyint] NULL,
	[oem_invoiced_by_org_level_code] [varchar](30) NULL,
	[customer_invoice_no] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[customer_invoice_date] [datetimeoffset](7) NULL,
	[invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_no] [tinyint] NULL,
	[invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_code] [varchar](30)NULL,
	[std_wty_template_id] [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	[std_wty_pm_applicable_ind] [bit] NULL,
	[std_wty_duration] [tinyint] NULL,
	[std_wty_duration_uom] [varchar](1) NULL,
	[std_wty_frequency_uom] [varchar](1) NULL,
	[std_wty_frequency] [numeric](5, 0) NULL,
	[std_wty_start_date] [datetimeoffset](7) NULL, 
	[std_wty_end_date] [datetimeoffset](7) NULL,
	[created_by_emp_id] [nvarchar](12) NOT NULL,
	[creation_date] [datetimeoffset](7) NOT NULL,
	[asset_location_country_code] [varchar](5) NULL,
	[asset_location_state_code] [nvarchar](10) NULL,
	[asset_location_district_code] [nvarchar](20) NULL,
	[udf_char_1] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_char_2] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_char_3] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_char_4] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_char_5] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_char_6] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_char_7] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_char_8] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_char_9] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_char_10] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[udf_float_1] [float] NULL,
	[udf_float_2] [float] NULL,
	[udf_float_3] [float] NULL,
	[udf_float_4] [float] NULL,
	[udf_date_1] [datetimeoffset](7) NULL,
	[udf_date_2] [datetimeoffset](7) NULL,
	[udf_date_3] [datetimeoffset](7) NULL,
	[udf_date_4] [datetimeoffset](7) NULL,
	[udf_analysis_code1] [nvarchar](20) NULL,
	[udf_analysis_code2] [nvarchar](20) NULL,
	[udf_analysis_code3] [nvarchar](20) NULL,
	[udf_analysis_code4] [nvarchar](20) NULL,
	[child_asset_id] [nvarchar](30) NULL,
	[child_equipment_id] [nvarchar](30) NULL,
	[child_equipment_oem] [nvarchar](60) NULL,
	[child_equipment_category] [nvarchar](30) NULL,
	[child_equipment_type] [nvarchar](30) NULL,
	[child_asset_status] [varchar](2) NULL
)

	declare asset_creation_cursor cursor for
	select company_id,country_code,asset_id,equipment_id,customer_id,customer_location_code,company_location_code,asset_category,asset_type,asset_status,additional_information,asset_location_code,locator_layout,servicing_org_level_no,servicing_org_level_code,installation_date,installation_job_ref_no,installation_by_org_level_no,installation_by_org_level_code,oem_invoice_no,oem_invoice_date,oem_invoiced_by_org_level_no,oem_invoiced_by_org_level_code,customer_invoice_no,customer_invoice_date,invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_no,invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_code,std_wty_template_id,std_wty_pm_applicable_ind,std_wty_duration,std_wty_duration_uom,std_wty_frequency,std_wty_start_date,std_wty_end_date,created_by_emp_id,creation_date,asset_location_country_code,asset_location_state_code,asset_location_district_code,udf_char_1,udf_char_2,udf_char_3,udf_char_4,udf_char_5,udf_char_6,udf_char_7,udf_char_8,udf_char_9,udf_char_10,udf_float_1,udf_float_2,udf_float_3,udf_float_4,udf_date_1,udf_date_2,udf_date_3,udf_date_4,udf_analysis_code1,udf_analysis_code2,udf_analysis_code3,udf_analysis_code4,std_wty_frequency_uom
	from #asset_master


		open asset_creation_cursor

		fetch next from asset_creation_cursor
		into @p_company_id,@p_country_code,@p_asset_id,@p_equipment_id,@p_customer_id,@p_customer_location_code,@p_company_location_code,@p_asset_category,@p_asset_type,@p_asset_status,@p_additional_information,@p_asset_location_code,@p_locator_layout,@p_servicing_org_level_no,@p_servicing_org_level_code,@p_installation_date,@p_installation_job_ref_no,@p_installation_by_org_level_no,@p_installation_by_org_level_code,@p_oem_invoice_no,@p_oem_invoice_date,@p_oem_invoiced_by_org_level_no,@p_oem_invoiced_by_org_level_code,@p_customer_invoice_no,@p_customer_invoice_date,@p_invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_no,@p_invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_code,@p_std_wty_template_id,@p_std_wty_pm_applicable_ind,@p_std_wty_duration,@p_std_wty_duration_uom,@p_std_wty_frequency,@p_std_wty_start_date,@p_std_wty_end_date,@p_created_by_emp_id,@p_creation_date,@p_asset_location_country_code,@p_asset_location_state_code,@p_asset_location_district_code,@p_udf_char_1,@p_udf_char_2,@p_udf_char_3,@p_udf_char_4,@p_udf_char_5,@p_udf_char_6,@p_udf_char_7,@p_udf_char_8,@p_udf_char_9,@p_udf_char_10,@p_udf_float_1,@p_udf_float_2,@p_udf_float_3,@p_udf_float_4,@p_udf_date_1,@p_udf_date_2,@p_udf_date_3,@p_udf_date_4,@p_udf_analysis_code1,@p_udf_analysis_code2,@p_udf_analysis_code3,@p_udf_analysis_code4,@p_std_wty_frequency_uom

		while @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
		begin

			set @p_user_id = 'jothi'
			set @p_locale_id = 'en-us'

			if not exists(select 1 from asset_master 
						  where company_id = @p_company_id 
						  and country_code = @p_country_code
						  and asset_id = @p_asset_id)

varchar(2))+'</invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_no><invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_code>'+@p_servicing_org_level_code+'</invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_code><std_wty_template_id>'+@p_std_wty_template_id+'</std_wty_template_id><std_wty_pm_applicable_ind>'+cast(@p_std_wty_pm_applicable_ind as nvarchar(2))+'</std_wty_pm_applicable_ind><std_wty_duration>'+cast(@p_std_wty_duration as nvarchar(20))+'</std_wty_duration><std_wty_duration_uom>'+@p_std_wty_duration_uom+'</std_wty_duration_uom><std_wty_frequency>'+cast(@p_std_wty_frequency as nvarchar(20))+'</std_wty_frequency><std_wty_frequency_uom>'+cast(@p_std_wty_frequency_uom as nvarchar(20))+'</std_wty_frequency_uom><std_wty_start_date>'+isnull(cast(@p_std_wty_start_date as varchar(24)),'')+'</std_wty_start_date><std_wty_end_date>'+isnull(cast(@p_std_wty_end_date as varchar(24)),'')+'</std_wty_end_date>', '<inputparam></inputparam>','A'

				 set @p_std_wty_start_date = ''
				 set @p_std_wty_end_date = ''

				  select @p_session_id = NEWID()

					SELECT	@o_update_status = ''
					SELECT	@errorNo = ''

					EXEC	@return_value = [dbo].[sp_save_manage_asset_master]
							@i_session_id = @p_session_id,
							@i_user_id = @p_user_id,
							@i_client_id = @p_company_id,
							@i_locale_id = @p_locale_id,
							@i_country_code = @p_country_code,
							@i_asset_id = @p_asset_id,
							@i_equipment_id = @p_equipment_id,
							@i_customer_id = @p_customer_id,
							@i_asset_location_code = @p_asset_location_code,
							@i_locator_layout = '',
							@i_installation_date = @p_installation_date,
							@i_asset_status = @p_asset_status,
							@i_org_level_no = @p_servicing_org_level_no,
							@i_org_level_code = @p_servicing_org_level_code,
							@i_rec_tstamp = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000',
							@i_inputparam_udf_xml = @p_inputparam_udf_xml,
							@i_save_mode = 'A',
							@o_update_status = @o_update_status OUTPUT,
							@inputparam_detail1 = @p_inputparam_detail1,
							@inputparam_detail2 = @p_inputparam_detail2,
							@inputparam_detail3 = @p_inputparam_detail3,
							@inputparam_detail4 = @p_inputparam_detail4,
							@inputparam_detail5 = @p_inputparam_detail5,
							@errorNo = @errorNo OUTPUT

					SELECT	@o_update_status as N'@o_update_status',
							@errorNo as N'@errorNo'

					SELECT	'Return Value' = @return_value


			end

		fetch next from asset_creation_cursor
		into @p_company_id,@p_country_code,@p_asset_id,@p_equipment_id,@p_customer_id,@p_customer_location_code,@p_company_location_code,@p_asset_category,@p_asset_type,@p_asset_status,@p_additional_information,@p_asset_location_code,@p_locator_layout,@p_servicing_org_level_no,@p_servicing_org_level_code,@p_installation_date,@p_installation_job_ref_no,@p_installation_by_org_level_no,@p_installation_by_org_level_code,@p_oem_invoice_no,@p_oem_invoice_date,@p_oem_invoiced_by_org_level_no,@p_oem_invoiced_by_org_level_code,@p_customer_invoice_no,@p_customer_invoice_date,@p_invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_no,@p_invoiced_to_customer_by_org_level_code,@p_std_wty_template_id,@p_std_wty_pm_applicable_ind,@p_std_wty_duration,@p_std_wty_duration_uom,@p_std_wty_frequency,@p_std_wty_start_date,@p_std_wty_end_date,@p_created_by_emp_id,@p_creation_date,@p_asset_location_country_code,@p_asset_location_state_code,@p_asset_location_district_code,@p_udf_char_1,@p_udf_char_2,@p_udf_char_3,@p_udf_char_4,@p_udf_char_5,@p_udf_char_6,@p_udf_char_7,@p_udf_char_8,@p_udf_char_9,@p_udf_char_10,@p_udf_float_1,@p_udf_float_2,@p_udf_float_3,@p_udf_float_4,@p_udf_date_1,@p_udf_date_2,@p_udf_date_3,@p_udf_date_4,@p_udf_analysis_code1,@p_udf_analysis_code2,@p_udf_analysis_code3,@p_udf_analysis_code4,@p_std_wty_frequency_uom

	end	
	close asset_creation_cursor
	deallocate asset_creation_cursor
